## <a name="windows-server-2003-extended-rights"></a><span data-ttu-id="21c6e-923">Direitos estendidos do Windows Server 2003</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="21c6e-923">Windows Server 2003 Extended Rights</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="21c6e-924">Essa classe contém os seguintes direitos estendidos para o Windows Server 2003:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="21c6e-924">This class contains the following extended rights for Windows Server 2003:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="21c6e-925">Nome comum</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="21c6e-925">Common Name</span></span>                                                                                              |
